the legal defense of set-off ( ऊपर ) थी originally introduced to prevent the अन्यायपूर्ण situation whereby a व्यक्ति ( `` Party a '' ) who owed money to another ( `` Party b '' ) could be भेजा to कर्जदार थाना, despite the fact कि पार्टी b also owed धन to पार्टी A.
the law thus allows both parties to defer payment until उनके respective दावा have महरूम सुना in court.
upon निर्णय, दोनो दावा are बुझे और replaced by a सिंगल जाल योग owing ( e.g. If Party a owes पार्टी b 100 और पार्टी b owes Party A 105, the two रकम हैं नियत off और replaced with a सिंगल obligation of 5 इससे पार्टी b to पार्टी a ).
set-off can also be incorporated by contractual agreement so कि, where a पार्टी मूलभूत, the mutual amounts owing are automatically नियत off और extinguished.
in certain jurisdictions ( including the UK ), set-off takes प्लेस automatically upon the insolvency of a कम्पनी.
इस अर्थात् कि, for each party जिससे is दोनो a creditor and debtor of the insolvent company, mutual debts are set-off विरूद्ध each अन्य, और तब either the bankrupt 's creditor can अर्जी the balance in the bankruptcy or the trustee in bankruptcy can पूछो for the संतुलन remaining to be paid, depending on which पक्ष owed the most.
इस has महरूम criticized as an undeclared security ब्याज that violates the principle of pari passu.
The alternative, जहाँ a creditor रै to अदा सब its debts, लकिन प्राप्त तभी a सीमित portion of the leftover moneys कि अन्य unsecured लेनदारों get, मुद्राएँ the danger of 'knock-on ' insolvencies.
the सही to नियत बंद is विशेषकर महत्वपूर्ण when रिपोर्टिंग a बैंको 's विकिरणों to regulatory अधिकारियों.
the situation where a बैंको has to रपट that it रै lent a विशाल योग to a borrower ( and is therefore exposed, because वहीँ is a रिस्क कि the borrower might डिफॉल्ट thereby leading to the loss of the bank 's or its depositors ' धन ) is thus replaced ( जहाँ the bank has लिया security over shares or प्रतिभूति of the borrower ) with an एक्सपोज़र of the money lent minus the मान of the security लिया.

conventional PCI ( PCI is an initialism formed from परिधीय Component Interconnect, part of the PCI लोकल Bus standard and often shortened to बस PCI ) is a लोकल computer bus for attaching hardware डिवाइस in a कंप्यूटर.
The पीसीआई bus supports the कृत्यों found on a processor bus, लकिन in a मानकीकृत format that is independent of any particular प्रोसेसर.
डिवाइस कनेक्ट to the bus appear to the प्रोसेसर to be connected सीधे to the प्रोसेसर बस, और are assigned addresses in the प्रोसेसर 's पता स्पेस.
संलग्न डिवाइस can लो either the रूप of an integrated circuit fitted onto the मदरबोर्ड itself, called a planar यंत्र in the पीसीआई specification, or an expansion card कि fits into a slot.
The पीसीआई लोकल बस was first implemented in IBM pc compatibles, where it विस्थापित the combination of ISA plus one VESA लोकल बस as the bus विन्यास.
it रै subsequently been adopted for other computer प्रकार.
पीसीआई और PCI-X हैं being replaced by PCI एक्स्प्रेस, but, सबसे motherboards हैं still बना साथ one or more PCI स्लॉट, which are sufficient लिये अनेक उपयोग.
The पीसीआई specification कवर the physical size of the बस ( including the size and spacing of the circuit फलक edge विद्युत सम्पर्क ), विद्युत विशेषताएँ, बस timing, और प्रोटोकॉल.
The specification can be खरीदा from the PCI Special ब्याज समूह ( PCI-SIG ).
Typical पीसीआई ताश प्रयुक्त in PCs include : संजाल ताश, ध्वनि cards, modems, अतिरिक्त ports such as usb or सीरियल, tv ट्यूनर ताश and disk controllers.
PCI वीडियो cards replaced isa and vesa cards, until growing bandwidth आवश्यकताएँ outgrew the capabilities of PCI ; the preferred interface लिये video cards became अगप, और then PCI एक्स्प्रेस.
PCI वीडियो ताश remain available for उपयोग साथ बूढ़ा pcs without AGP or PCI Express slots.
अनेक devices previously provided on PCI विस्तार ताश are अभी commonly integrated onto motherboards or available in universal सीरियल bus और पीसीआई Express versions.
Caffeine is a कड़वा, white crystalline xanthine alkaloid that acts as a stimulant drug.
कैफीन is found in varying quantities in the seeds, leaves, और fruit of कुछ plants, जहाँ it अधिनियमों as a natural pesticide कि paralyzes and मारता निश्चित कीट feeding on the plants, as well as बढ़ाना the बदला मेमोरी of pollinators.
It is most commonly खपत by humans in infusions निकाली इससे the बीज of the coffee संयंत्र और the leaves of the tea bush, as well as इससे विभिन्न भोजन और पेय containing products निकला from the कोला nut.
Other स्त्रोत include yerba maté, guarana berries, guayusa, और the yaupon होली.
In humans, caffeine अधिनियमों as a सेंट्रल nervous प्रणाली उत्तेजक, temporarily warding बंद drowsiness और restoring alertness.
it is the संसार 's सबसे widely खपत psychoactive drug, but unlike many अन्य psychoactive substances, it is legal और unregulated in nearly सब भाग of the संसार.
पेय containing caffeine, such as coffee, tea, soft पेय, और energy पेय, enjoy ग्रेट popularity.
in North अमेरिका, 90 % of adults consume कैफीन रोज़.
भाग of the reason कैफीन is वर्गीकृत by the Food और Drug Administration as GRAS ( generally पहचाना as सुरक्षित ) is that विषाक्त doses ( over 10 grams ) are much उच्चतर than typically used doses ( कम than 500 milligrams ).
ordinary consumption can have कम health risks, भी जब carried on लिये सालो – वहीँ may be a modest सुरक्षात्मक प्रभाव विरूद्ध some diseases, including parkinsons बीमारी, और निश्चित प्रकार of कर्कट.
कैफीन can have both positive and negative effects on चिंता disorders.

कैफीन has pressor and mild diuretic प्रभाव जब administered to people जो are नहीं प्रयुक्त to it, but regular users develop a सहिष्णुता to इस प्रभाव, and studies have generally विफल to support the common notion कि ordinary खपत contributes significantly to निर्जलीकरण.

The degree to which कैफीन can उपज clinically significant शारीरिक और mental dependence remains a विषय of controversy in the चिकित्सा literature.

John fitzgerald `` जोकर '' कैनेडी ( May 29, 1917 – November 22, 1963 ), often referred to by his आद्याक्षर jfk, was the 35th अध्यक्ष of the संयुक्त राज्य, serving from 1961 जबतक उसके death in 1963.
बाद सैन्य service as कमांडर of the मोटर torpedo नौकाएँ pt-109 और PT-59 during संसार War II in the दक्षिण Pacific, कैनेडी represented Massachusetts ' 11th congressional district in the u.S. House of Representatives from 1947 to 1953 as a Democrat.
Thereafter, he served in the U.S. Senate इससे 1953 until 1960.
Kennedy defeated वाइस अध्यक्ष और Republican candidate रिचर्ड Nixon in the 1960 u.S. presidential election.

the कैनेडी administration adopted the नीति of the रणनीतिक Hamlet कार्यक्रम which थी implemented by the दक्षिण Vietnamese सरकारी.

a Fire Alarm कंट्रोल फलक ( FACP ), or आग सचेतक कंट्रोल Unit ( facu ), is the controlling घटक of a आग सचेतक प्रणाली.

the world’s first ice-calorimeter, प्रयुक्त in the शीत of 1782-83, by एंटोनी Lavoisier and Pierre-Simon Laplace, to determine the ऊष्मा involved in various रासायनिक परिवर्तन ; calculations which were based on जोसेफ ब्लैक ’s prior डिस्कवरी of अदृश्य heat.
These प्रयोग चिह्नित the foundation of thermochemistry.
a ऊष्मामापी ( इससे लैटिन calor, meaning heat ) is an object प्रयुक्त लिये calorimetry, or the प्रक्रम of measuring the ऊष्मा of रासायनिक reactions or physical परिवर्तन as well as heat capacity.
Differential स्कैनिंग calorimeters, समतापी microcalorimeters, titration calorimeters और त्वरित रेट calorimeters are among the सबसे आम types.
A सरल calorimeter just consists of a thermometer संलग्न to a मेटल संग्राहक full of जल suspended ऊपर a combustion कक्ष.

the law of सामान्य average is a legal principle of maritime law according to which all पार्टियों in a समुद्र venture proportionally share कोई losses resulting from a voluntary sacrifice of part of the ship or cargo to save the पूरे in an emergency.
in the exigencies of जोखिमों faced at समुद्र, क्रू सदस्यों often have अनमोल little समय in which to determine precisely whose कार्गो वे हैं jettisoning.
Thus, to avoid quarrelling that could बर्बाद मूल्यवान time, वहीँ arose the equitable अभ्यास whereby all the व्यापारियों जिनकी cargo landed सकुशल would be पुकारा on to योगदान a portion, based upon a share or percentage, to the merchant or merchants whose goods था been tossed overboard to avert निकट peril.

The पहला codification of general औसत was the यॉर्क Antwerp नियम of 1890.
अमरीकी कंपनियाँ स्वीकृत it in 1949.
General average requires three तत्व which हैं clearly stated by Mr. इंसाफ grier in बर्नार्ड v. आदमs:
`` 1st.
a common danger : a खतरे in जिससे पोत, कार्गो और क्रू सब participate ; a danger निकट और apparently 'inevitable, ' except by voluntarily रूष्ट the loss of a portion of the पूरे to save the शेष. ''
`` 2nd. वहीँ जरूर be a voluntary jettison, jactus, or ढलाई away, of some portion of the joint चिंता for the purpose of avoiding this निकट peril, periculi imminentis evitandi causa, or, in अन्य words, a transfer of the peril इससे the whole to a particular portion of the whole. ''
`` 3rd.
This attempt to avoid the निकट आम peril must be कामयाब ''.

an oled ( सशुल्क light-emitting डायोड ) is a light-emitting डायोड ( led ) in which the emissive electroluminescent layer is a film of सशुल्क यौगिक which emits light in response to an electric current.
इस layer of organic सेमीकंडक्टर is situated between दो electrodes.
generally, at तनिक one of ये electrodes is transparent.
OLEDs are used to बनाएँ digital displays in डिवाइस such as television screens, कंप्यूटर मॉनीटर, पोर्टेबल प्रणालियों such as mobile phones, हैंडहेल्ड games consoles and गुस्से.
a major area of शोध is the development of श्वेत oled devices for उपयोग in solid-state lighting अनुप्रयोग.
There are two प्रमुख परिवारों of oleds : those based on छोटी molecules और those employing polymers.
Adding mobile ions to an oled creates a light-emitting electrochemical कोशिका or LEC, which has a slightly अलग विधि of operation.
oled displays can उपयोग either passive-matrix ( PMOLED ) or active-matrix संबोधित schemes.
Active-matrix oleds ( amoled ) require a thin-film ट्रांजिस्टर backplane to switch प्रत्येक व्यक्तिगत pixel on or off, but allow लिये उच्चतर resolution और larger प्रदर्शक आकार.
an oled display works बगैर a backlight.
Thus, it can प्रदर्शक गहन black स्तर and can be thinner और हल्का than a द्रव क्रिस्टल प्रदर्शक ( LCD ).
in low ambient लाइट conditions ऐसे as a dark room an oled स्क्रीन can achieve a उच्चतर कंट्रास्ट ratio than an एलसीडी, whether the LCD uses ठंडा कैथोड fluorescent lamps or LED backlight.

It is made by placing uncooked filling typically of meat and vegetables, without मांस in शाकाहारी संस्करण, on a flat pastry circle and folding it to wrap the filling, crimping the किनारे to रूप a seal.
बाद बेकिंग, the result is a raised semicircular comestible.
The traditional cornish pasty, जिससे रै सुरक्षित Geographical Indication ( PGI ) औकात in Europe, is filled with beef, sliced or diced आलू, swede ( भी known as a yellow turnip or rutabaga – referred to in Cornwall as turnip ) और प्याज, seasoned with salt और pepper, and is baked.
आज, the pasty is the food most संबद्ध with कॉर्नवॉल, it is regarded as the national dish, और it accounts for 6 % of the Cornish खाना अर्थव्यवस्था.
pasties with many different fillings हैं बना ; some दुकानें specialise in selling all sorts of pasties.
the origins of the pasty are unclear, हालांकि वहीँ are many सन्दर्भ to them throughout ऐतिहासिक documents and fiction.
The pasty is now popular world-wide due to the spread of cornish miners, और variations can be मिला in Australia, the संयुक्त राज्य, मैक्सिको और elsewhere.

It is, however, constantly active at a basic level to maintain homeostasis.
सुरक्षित Digital or ( sd ) is a non-volatile memory card स्वरूप for उपयोग in पोर्टेबल devices, ऐसे as mobile phones, डिजिटल cameras, GPS नेविगेशन डिवाइस, and tablet कंप्यूटर.

sd technologies have महरूम implemented in अधिक than 400 brands across दर्जनों of उत्पाद categories और more than 8,000 मॉडल.
the Secure डिजिटल format शामिल चार card families available in three अलग रूप कारकों.
the चार परिवारों हैं the असली standard-capacity ( SDSC ), the high-capacity ( sdhc ), the eXtended-Capacity ( sdxc ), और the sdio, जिससे combines input/output functions with आंकड़ा भंडार.
The तीन रूप कारकों are the original आकार, the `` मिनी '' आकार, और the `` micro '' आकार ( see उदाहरण ).
There are अनेक combinations of form factors और device families.
electrically passive adapters allow the उपयोग of a छोटी card in a host यंत्र built to hold a larger कार्ड.
मेजबान devices that comply साथ newer versions of the specification provide पिछड़ा संगतता और accept older sd cards, but इस आलेख explains several factors कि can prevent the उपयोग of a newer sd card:
a नए कार्ड may प्रस्ताव greater क्षमता than the host device can हैंडल.
A newer card may use a संचिका प्रणाली the मेजबान यंत्र can not navigate.
उपयोग of an SDIO कार्ड requires the मेजबान device be designed for the input/output functions the कार्ड provides.
The संगठन of the कार्ड थी बदला starting with the sdhc परिवार.
कुछ vendors produced SDSC ताश above 1 gb पहले the sda था मानकीकृत a विधि of doing so.

विटामिन d is a समूह of fat-soluble secosteroids जिम्मेदार for intestinal अवशोषण of calcium and फास्फेट.
In humans, the most महत्वपूर्ण सम्बन्धित compounds of vitamin D हैं vitamin d2 और vitamin d3.

an सशुल्क रासायनिक यौगिक ( or related set of यौगिकों ) is तभी scientifically पुकारा a vitamin जब it can not be synthesized in sufficient quantities by an organism, and जरूर be obtained इससे their आहार.

In the जिगर vitamin D is परिवर्तित to calcidiol, which is also known as calcifediol ( INN ), 25-hydroxycholecalciferol, or 25-hydroxyvitamin d—abbreviated 25 ( OH ) d ; और जिससे is the विशिष्ट विटामिन d metabolite कि is measured in serum to determine a व्यक्ति 's vitamin D status.

Standard form of the आवधिक तालिका.
The रंगों represent अलग श्रेणी of तत्व समझाया नीचे.
The आवधिक तालिका is a tabular प्रदर्शक of the रासायनिक तत्व, व्यवस्थित on the आधार of their atomic numbers, इलेक्ट्रॉन configurations, और recurring chemical properties.
Elements हैं प्रस्तुत in order of increasing परमाणु क्रमांक ( क्रमांक of protons ).
the standard रूप of तालिका comprises an 18 × 7 grid or main देह of तत्व, positioned ऊपर a smaller double पंक्ति of तत्व.
the table can also be deconstructed into चार rectangular blocks : the s-block to the left, the p-block to the right, the d-block in the मध्य, and the f-block नीचे that.
The पंक्ति of the तालिका are called periods ; the columns of the s-, d-, and p-blocks हैं पुकारा groups, साथ some of these having names ऐसे as the हैलोजन्स or the noble gases.
चूंकि, by परिभाषा, a periodic table incorporates recurring रुझान, कोई such table can be प्रयुक्त to derive relationships between the गुण of the तत्व and भविष्यवाणी the properties of new, yet to be discovered or synthesized, तत्व.
as a result, a periodic table—whether in the मानक रूप or कुछ अन्य variant—provides a उपयोगी फ्रेमवर्क लिये analyzing रासायनिक behavior, and such टेबल हैं widely used in chemistry and अन्य sciences.
Although precursors मौजूद, Dmitri mendeleev is generally credited साथ the publication, in 1869, of the पहला widely पहचाना आवधिक table.
He विकसित उसके तालिका to illustrate periodic रुझान in the गुण of the then-known elements.
mendeleev also पूर्वानुमानित some गुण of then-unknown elements that होता be expected to fill gaps in this तालिका.
सबसे of उसके पूर्वानुमान यहूद proved correct when the तत्व in question यहूद subsequently discovered.
Mendeleev 's आवधिक तालिका has चूंकि been विस्तारित and refined with the discovery or संश्लेषण of further नई elements और the विकास of नई theoretical मॉडल to बताइये chemical बर्ताव.
सब elements from atomic संख्याएँ 1 ( हाइड्रोजन ) to 118 ( ununoctium ) have been खोजा or synthesized.
the elements from 1 to 98 ( californium ) have महरूम found to exist naturally, although some हैं मिला तभी in trace amounts और यहूद initially discovered by synthesis in laboratories.
the तत्व बाद 98 have only महरूम synthesized in laboratories.
उत्पादन of elements beyond ununoctium is being धड़ा, with the सवाल of कैसा the periodic तालिका may need to be modified to accommodate कोई ऐसे additions being a पदार्थ of जारी debate.
numerous सिंथेटिक radionuclides of naturally occurring तत्व have भी been उत्पादित in laboratories.

The United States of America ( USA or U.S.A. ), commonly पुकारा the United राज्य ( us or U.S. ) or अमेरिका, is a federal republic consisting of पचास राज्य और a federal ज़िला.

The देश भी रै पाँच populated और नौ unpopulated territories in the Pacific और the caribbean.
At 3.79 लाख वर्गाकार मील ( 9.83 लाख km2 ) and with around 315 लाख people, the संयुक्त राज्य is the third- or fourth-largest देश by कुल area and the third-largest by both land area और जनसांख्यिकी.
It is एक of the संसार 's most ethnically diverse and multicultural राष्ट्र, the product of large-scale immigration इससे many देशों.
the भूगोल and climate of the u.S. is भी extremely विविध, साथ रेगिस्तान, plains, वनों, and mountains that are home to a चौड़ी variety of species.
paleoindians migrated इससे एशिया to what is now the United States मेनलैंड around 15,000 years ago.
After 1500, Old संसार diseases introduced by Europeans greatly घटाया उनके populations.
European colonization began around 1600 और आए ज़्यादातर from इंग्लैण्ड.
The United राज्य उभरा इससे thirteen British colonies located along the अटलांटिक seaboard.
Disputes between ग्रेट ब्रिटेन and the American colonies led to the अमरीकी Revolution.
on July 4, 1776, delegates इससे the 13 colonies unanimously जारी the घोषणा of Independence, जिससे established the संयुक्त States of America.
the American क्रांतिकारी War, which ended with the recognition of independence of the संयुक्त राज्य इससे the Kingdom of ग्रेट ब्रिटेन, थी the first कामयाब युद्ध of independence against a यूरोपीय औपनिवेशिक साम्राज्य.
the वर्तमान Constitution थी अपनाया on सितंबर 17, 1787 ; twenty-seven Amendments have चूंकि महरूम added to the संविधान.
the first टेन amendments, collectively named the Bill of अधिकारों, were ratified in 1791 और guarantee many fundamental सिविल अधिकारों and freedoms.
Driven by the doctrine of manifest नियति, the United राज्य embarked on a vigorous expansion across North अमेरिका throughout the 19th century.
इस शामिल displacing native जनजातियों, acquiring नई territories, और gradually admitting new राज्य.
The American सिविल War ended legalized गुलामी in the संयुक्त States.

The baptism of Jesus marks the शुरूआत of उसके public मंत्रालय.

The baptismal झाँकी शामिल the आकाश opening, a dove-like descent of the Holy स्पिरिट, और a voice इससे heaven saying, `` इस is my beloved बेटे, in whom I am खूब प्रसन्न. ''

Methylcobalamin ( दिखाया ) is a रूप of vitamin b12.

Vitamin b12, विटामिन B12 or विटामिन B-12, भी पुकारा cobalamin, is a water-soluble विटामिन साथ a key भूमिका in the सामान्य functioning of the brain and बेचैन प्रणाली, and लिये the गठन of blood.

It is normally involved in the चयापचय of every कोशिका of the इंसान देह, especially affecting DNA संश्लेषण और विनियमन, लकिन also fatty एसिड synthesis and energy production.

Only bacteria and आर्किया have the enzymes required लिये its संश्लेषण, हालांकि many foods हैं a प्राकृतिक source of b12 because of बैक्टीरियल symbiosis.
The विटामिन is the largest और most structurally complicated vitamin और can be उत्पादित industrially only through bacterial fermentation-synthesis.
Vitamin b12 consists of a क्लास of chemically related compounds ( vitamers ), सब of जिससे have vitamin activity.
it contains the biochemically विरल element कोबाल्ट.
Biosynthesis of the basic structure of the विटामिन is accomplished तभी by bacteria ( which प्रायः produce hydroxocobalamin ), लकिन conversion between different फ़ॉर्म of the vitamin can be संपन्नता in the इंसान body.
a आम semi-synthetic रूप of the vitamin, cyanocobalamin, करता not occur in प्रकृति, लकिन is produced from बैक्टीरियल hydroxocobalamin और then प्रयुक्त in अनेक दवाएँ and पूरक, and as a food additive, because of इसके स्थिरता और निम्नतर production cost.
In the body it is परिवर्तित to the इंसान physiological forms methylcobalamin और adenosylcobalamin, leaving पीछे the cyanide, albeit in minimal concentration.
More recently, hydroxocobalamin, methylcobalamin, and adenosylcobalamin can be मिला in more expensive pharmacological products और खाना supplements.
the अतिरिक्त utility of these is currently debated.
विटामिन b12 थी खोजा इससे its संबंध to the बीमारी pernicious रक्ताल्पता, which is an असंक्राम्य disease in which parietal cells of the stomach जिम्मेदार लिये secreting intrinsic factor are destroyed.
Intrinsic factor is crucial लिये the सामान्य absorption of B12, so a lack of मूलभूत फ़ैक्टर, as seen in घातक रक्ताल्पता, कल्याणकारी a विटामिन B12 कमियां.
अनेक अन्य subtler kinds of विटामिन b12 कमियां and उनके biochemical प्रभाव have चूंकि been elucidated.

the colonial इतिहास of the संयुक्त States कवर the इतिहास of European settlements from the प्रारंभ of colonization of America जबतक their incorporation into the United राज्य.
In the लेट 16th century, England, France, Spain और the Netherlands शुभारम्भ प्रमुख colonization programs in eastern उत्तर अमेरिका.
Small जल्दी attempts—such as the अंग्रेज़ी खोया Colony of roanoke —often disappeared ; everywhere the death रेट of the पहला arrivals was बहुत ऊँची.
nevertheless successful colonies यहूद established.
यूरोपीय settlers came इससे a किस्में of सोशल and religious groups.
No aristocrats settled permanently, लकिन a क्रमांक of adventurers, soldiers, किसानो, and tradesmen arrived.
Diversity was an American characteristic as the Dutch of New Netherland, the Swedes and finns of नई Sweden, the English Quakers of पेन्सिलवेनिया, the अंग्रेज़ी puritans of New इंग्लैण्ड, the English settlers of jamestown, and the `` worthy ग़रीब '' of जॉर्जिया, came to the new महाद्वीप and built colonies with distinctive सोशल, religious, political and आर्थिक styles.
occasionally एक colony took control of another ( दौरान wars between their यूरोपीय अभिभावक ).
Only in Nova स्कोटिया ( now भाग of कनाडा ) did the conquerors expel the previous colonists.
बजाय they सब lived side by side in peace.
वहीँ यहूद no प्रमुख civil wars among the 13 colonies, and the two मुख्य armed rebellions ( in Virginia in 1676 और in नई York in 1689–91 ) यहूद short-lived असफलताओं.

इस ग्रेट वृत्त divides the sphere, e.g. the धरती, into दो बांटती.

gerardus Mercator in उसके Atlas cosmographicae ( 1595 ) uses a prime मध्याह्न somewhere close to 25°w, passing बस to the west of Santa Maria द्वीप in the Atlantic.
His 180th मध्याह्न runs साथ the जलसन्धि of anián ( Bering जलसन्धि )

This article deals साथ medicine as practiced by प्रशिक्षित पेशेवर इससे प्राचीन टाइम्स to the उपस्थित.
The प्राचीन Egyptians had a प्रणाली of medicine that was very उन्नत लिये इसके time और influenced बाद चिकित्सा traditions.
The उन्होंने और babylonians दोनो introduced the concepts of निदान, prognosis, and चिकित्सा examination.
The Greeks गई भी further, and उन्नत as खूब medical ethics.
the hippocratic Oath, स्टिल लिया by डॉक्टर today, was written in यूनानियों in the 5th सदी BCE.
In the medieval era, surgical practices inherited from the प्राचीन मास्टर्स यहूद improved and तब systematized in Rogerius 's The अभ्यास of सर्जरी.

the रोगाणु theory of disease in the 19th century led to cures for many संक्रामक diseases.
Military doctors उन्नत the विधि of trauma treatment and सर्जरी.
Public स्वास्थ्य measures were developed especially in the 19th century as the rapid growth of शहरों जरूरी व्यवस्थित sanitary measures.
Advanced शोध centers opened in the early 20th सदी, प्रायः connected साथ प्रमुख अस्पताल.
The mid-20th century was characterized by new biological उपचार, such as एंटीबायोटिक.

आयुर्विज्ञान was heavily professionalized in the 20th सदी, और new careers opened to महिलाओं as नर्स ( from the 1870s ) और as physicians ( विशेषकर after 1970 ).
the 21st century is characterized by बहुत उन्नत research involving numerous fields of विज्ञान.

Potassium is a रासायनिक element साथ प्रतीक K ( from neo-latin kalium ) और atomic क्रमांक 19.
elemental potassium is a नरम silvery-white क्षारीय metal that oxidizes rapidly in एयर और is बहुत reactive साथ water, generating sufficient heat to ignite the हाइड्रोजन emitted in the प्रतिक्रिया and burning with a lilac ज्वाला.
क्युकी पोटैशियम और सोडियम are chemically very समान, their लवण यहूद not at first differentiated.
The अस्तित्व of अनेक elements in उनके लवण थी suspected इससे 1702, और this थी सिद्ध in 1807 when potassium और sodium यहूद individually पृथक इससे different salts by electrolysis.
Potassium in nature occurs तभी in ionic लवण.
as such, it is मिला dissolved in seawater ( which is 0.04 % potassium by वज़न ), and is भाग of many minerals.
Most औद्योगिक chemical applications of potassium employ the अपेक्षाकृत ऊँची घुलनशीलता in जल of पोटैशियम compounds, such as पोटैशियम soaps.
पोटैशियम metal has only a few special applications, होने replaced in most chemical reactions साथ सोडियम मेटल.
Potassium ions are जरुरी for the function of सब जीना कोशिकाएं.
Potassium आयन diffusion is a key mechanism in तंत्रिका transmission, and पोटैशियम depletion in animals, सहित humans, results in विभिन्न हृदय डिस्फंक्शन.
Potassium accumulates in plant cells, और यूँ fresh फल और सब्जियां हैं a good dietary source of it.
Conversely, most plants except specialist halophytes are intolerant of salt, और sodium is उपस्थित in them तभी in low विशेषज्ञता.
इस resulted in पोटैशियम first होने पृथक from potash, the ashes of plants, giving the तत्व इसके नाम.
लिये the same कारण, भारी crop production rapidly depletes soils of potassium, and agricultural fertilizers consume 95 % of global potassium रासायनिक उत्पादन.

A superhero ( sometimes rendered super-hero or सुपर नायिका ) is a type of stock character possessing `` असाधारण or superhuman powers '' और dedicated to protecting the public.

सर थामस अधिक ( ; 7 February 14786 जुलाई 1535 ), ज्ञात to रोमन Catholics as संत थामस More since 1935, थी an अंग्रेज़ी lawyer, सोशल philosopher, लेखक, statesman, and विख्यात पुनर्जागरण humanist.
He was an important पार्षद to Henry viii of इंग्लैण्ड and was Lord Chancellor from October 1529 to 16 May 1532.
he थी canonized by पोप Pius xi in 1935 as one of the early martyrs of the schism that separated the गिरिजाघर of England from रोम in the 16th century.
In 2000, पोप जॉन पॉल ii declared उसे संरक्षक of कैथोलिक statesmen और politicians.
More थी an opponent of the Protestant reformation, in particular of Martin Luther and विलियम टिंडेल.
However, since 1980, he is भी commemorated by the Church of England as a reformation वीरगति.
More coined the शब्द `` यूटोपिया `` – a name he gave to the ideal and imaginary island nation, the political system of जिससे he वर्णित in Utopia, published in 1516.
He opposed the किंग 's separation इससे the रोमन Catholic Church और refused to accept उसे as Supreme सिर of the Church of इंग्लैण्ड, a शीर्षक जिससे had been given by पार्लियामेंट through the अधिनियम of Supremacy of 1534.

In 1535, he was आजमाया for treason, convicted on perjured testimony, और beheaded.

वहीँ थी a अधिक विवादास्पद side to अधिक 's life, क्युकी he advocated the persecution and निष्पादन of protestants who refused to recant their faith.
However, the निर्णय of history रै महरूम largely willing to forgive this in लाइट of the times he lived in and उसके martyrdom in the रोमन Catholic कारण.

Acoustic coupler मॉडेम
A मॉडेम ( modulator-demodulator ) is a यंत्र कि modulates an एनालॉग carrier सिग्नल to encode डिजिटल information, and भी demodulates such a carrier सिग्नल to decode the transmitted information.
The goal is to उपज a signal कि can be transmitted easily और decoded to reproduce the असली digital आंकड़ा.
Modems can be used over any means of transmitting analog signals, from लाइट emitting diodes to रेडियो.
The most familiar उदाहरण is a voice band मॉडेम that turns the डिजिटल आंकड़ा of a निजी कंप्यूटर into modulated electrical signals in the voice आवृत्ति range of a telephone चैनल.
ये सिग्नल can be transmitted over telephone लाइनों और demodulated by another modem at the receiver side to रिकवर the डिजिटल data.
modems हैं generally classified by the amount of data they can भेजें in a दिए unit of समय, प्रायः expressed in बिट्स प्रति second ( bit/s, or bps ), or bytes प्रति second ( b/s ).
Modems can alternatively be classified by उनके symbol रेट, measured in baud.
The baud unit denotes symbols per दूसरी, or the number of टाइम्स per second the मॉडेम sends a new सिग्नल.
लिये उदाहरण, the ITU v.21 standard used audio frequency shift keying साथ दो possible बारंबारता corresponding to दो पृथक symbols ( or एक बिट per प्रतीक ), to carry 300 बिट्स per दूसरी using 300 baud.
by contrast, the original itu V.22 मानक, which थी समर्थ to transmit और receive चार पृथक symbols ( two bits प्रति symbol ), handled 1,200 bit/s by sending 600 symbols प्रति second ( 600 baud ) using phase शिफ़्ट keying.
The Declaration of Independence is a बयान adopted by the महाद्वीपीय Congress on July 4, 1776, which घोषित that the thirteen अमरीकी colonies, then at युद्ध साथ ग्रेट Britain, regarded themselves as स्वतंत्र राज्य, और no longer a part of the अंग्रेजों Empire.
बजाय वे now formed a new nation—the संयुक्त राज्य of America.
जॉन एडम्स was a leader in pushing लिये independence, which थी unanimously स्वीकृत on जुलाई 2.
a committee था already drafted the औपचारिक घोषणा, to be तैयार जब कॉंग्रेस voted on स्वतंत्रता.
एडम्स persuaded the committee to select Thomas Jefferson to compose the असली draft of the दस्तावेज़, जिससे कॉंग्रेस would संपादन to उपज the फाइनल version.
The घोषणा थी ultimately a औपचारिक explanation of why कॉंग्रेस था voted on जुलाई 2 to घोषित स्वतंत्रता from Great Britain, more than a साल बाद the outbreak of the अमरीकी Revolutionary War.
the national जन्मदिवस, the Independence दिन is celebrated on July 4, although एडम्स wanted जुलाई 2.
बाद ratifying the टेक्स्ट on July 4, Congress issued the घोषणा of स्वतंत्रता in अनेक फ़ॉर्म.
It was initially published as the printed Dunlap broadside that was widely वितरित और पढ़ा to the public.
the most प्रसिद्ध संस्करण of the घोषणा, a हस्ताक्षरित नक़ल कि is popularly regarded as the घोषणा of स्वतंत्रता, is displayed at the National Archives in Washington, d.c.
Although the wording of the घोषणा थी स्वीकृत on July 4, the date of its signing थी August 2.
The original जुलाई 4 संयुक्त States घोषणा of स्वतंत्रता manuscript थी खोया while all अन्य नक़ल have महरूम निकला इससे this असली दस्तावेज़.
the स्त्रोत और interpretation of the घोषणा have been the विषय of much scholarly inquiry.
the Declaration justified the स्वतंत्रता of the संयुक्त राज्य by listing औपनिवेशिक grievances विरूद्ध किंग George III, और by asserting निश्चित प्राकृतिक and legal rights, including a right of क्रान्ति.
having परोसा its original purpose in announcing independence, the text of the घोषणा was initially उपेक्षित बाद the अमरीकी क्रान्ति.
Since then, it has come to be माना a प्रमुख बयान on human rights, विशेषकर its second sentence:
We hold these सच्चाई to be self-evident, कि all मेन हैं created equal, that they are endowed by their निर्माता with certain unalienable Rights, कि among ये are Life, Liberty और the pursuit of Happiness.
This रै been called `` एक of the best-known sentences in the English भाषा '', containing `` the most potent and consequential words in अमरीकी इतिहास. ''
The passage आए to represent a moral मानक to which the संयुक्त States should strive.
इस दृश्य was notably promoted by Abraham Lincoln, जो माना the घोषणा to be the foundation of उसके political philosophy, और argued कि the घोषणा is a statement of सिद्धान्त through जिससे the संयुक्त राज्य Constitution should be interpreted.
It has inspired work for the rights of अधिकारहीन लोगों throughout the world.

हाइड्रोजन is a chemical element साथ प्रतीक H and परमाणु number 1.
साथ an atomic weight of ( for hydrogen-1 ), hydrogen is the lightest तत्व and its monatomic form ( h1 ) is the most abundant chemical substance, constituting roughly 75 % of the Universe 's baryonic mass.
non- remnant stars are mainly composed of हाइड्रोजन in its plasma state.
at standard temperature और दबाव, हाइड्रोजन is a colorless, odorless, tasteless, non-toxic, nonmetallic, अत्यधिक combustible diatomic गैस साथ the molecular formula H2.
सबसे of the हाइड्रोजन on धरती is in अणुओं ऐसे as water and सशुल्क यौगिकों क्युकी हाइड्रोजन readily forms covalent compounds with most non-metallic तत्व.
हाइड्रोजन plays a particularly important role in acid-base chemistry साथ अनेक reactions exchanging protons between soluble अणुओं.
in ionic compounds, it can लो a negative charge ( an anion known as a hydride और written as H− ), or as a positively चार्ज species H+.
The latter cation is written as हालांकि composed of a bare प्रोटॉन, but in reality, hydrogen cations in ionic compounds सदा occur as अधिक complex species.
the सबसे common isotope of hydrogen is protium ( name rarely used, symbol 1h ) with a single proton और no neutrons.
as the सरलतम अणु ज्ञात, the हाइड्रोजन अणु has महरूम of theoretical उपयोग.

Visualization of fragmentation and तब of defragmentation
In the maintenance of file प्रणालियों, defragmentation is a प्रक्रम कि reduces the राशि of fragmentation.
It करता this by physically organizing the contents of the द्रव्यमान भंडार device used to स्टोर files into the smallest number of contiguous regions ( fragments ).
it भी attempts to बनाएँ larger regions of फ़्री स्पेस using compaction to impede the वापसी of fragmentation.
कुछ defragmentation utilities try to keep छोटी फाइलें भीतर a सिंगल directory together, as वे are प्रायः accessed in sequence.
Defragmentation is लाभदायक और relevant to file प्रणालियों on electromechanical disk drives.
The movement of the hard ड्राइव 's read/write heads over अलग क्षेत्रों of the disk जब accessing fragmented files is slower, compared to accessing the संपूर्ण सामग्री of a non-fragmented संचिका sequentially without moving the read/write heads to seek other fragments.
a service-level अनुबंध ( sla ) is a part of a service contract where a सेवा is formally defined.
In practice, the term sla is sometimes used to refer to the contracted डिलीवरी time ( of the service or performance ).

utilization management is the मूल्यांकन of the appropriateness, medical need and दक्षता of स्वास्थ्य care services प्रक्रियाओं और सुविधाएं according to established मापदण्ड or दिशानिर्देश and under the प्रावधानों of an applicable स्वास्थ्य benefits योजना.
Typically it includes new क्रियाएँ or decisions based upon the analysis of a case.
Utilization प्रबन्धन describes proactive procedures, including discharge नियोजन, concurrent नियोजन, pre-certification और नैदानिक case appeals.
It also covers proactive प्रक्रियाओं, such as संयुक्त नैदानिक समीक्षाएँ and peer reviews, as well as appeals introduced by the प्रदाता, payer or patient.
As pre-certification और संयुक्त review of cases grew, utilization प्रबन्धन spun आउट of utilization review.
जबकि नहीं synonymous, स्वास्थ्य परवाह professionals tend to उपयोग the terms as interchangeable.
the difference is utilization management is और intends to manage स्वास्थ्य care मामले efficiently और लागत effectively पहले and दौरान health care प्रशासन.
Utilization review is more considering whether health परवाह was appropriately लागू after it was administered.
There हैं four मौलिक तकनीकों in utilization management:
माँग प्रबन्धन
utilization Review
Case प्रबन्धन
बीमारी प्रबन्धन

The United राज्य House of प्रतिनिधि is एक of the दो घरों of the United राज्य कॉंग्रेस ( a bicameral legislature ).

a बंद up picture of a गैंडा स्किन.
स्किन is the soft outer covering of vertebrates.
Other एनिमल coverings ऐसे as the arthropod exoskeleton have different developmental origin, ढांचा and रासायनिक composition.
The adjective cutaneous means `` of the स्किन '' ( from Latin cutis, स्किन ).
In स्तनधारियों, the skin is the largest organ of the integumentary system made up of अनेक layers of ectodermal ऊतक, और गार्ड the underlying muscles, bones, ligaments और आतंरिक अंगों.
स्किन of a अलग प्रकृति exists in amphibians, सरीसृपों, and पक्षियों.
All mammals have some बाल on उनके skin, even marine स्तनधारियों which appear to be hairless.
The skin interfaces साथ the पर्यावरण and is the पहला लकीर of defense from external factors.
लिये उदाहरण, the skin plays a कुंजी भूमिका in protecting the देह against pathogens and excessive जल घाटा.
Its other कृत्यों हैं insulation, temperature regulation, sensation, and the production of विटामिन D folates.
Severely damaged skin may heal by forming scar tissue.
इस is sometimes discoloured और depigmented.
The thickness of स्किन भी varies इससे location to location on an organism.
in इंसानो लिये उदाहरण, the skin स्तिथ अंतर्गत the eyes और around the eyelids is the thinnest स्किन in the देह at 0.5 mm मोटा, और is one of the first क्षेत्रों to दिखाएँ लक्षण of aging such as `` crows feet '' और wrinkles.
the स्किन on the palms and the soles of the feet is 4 mm मोटा and the thickest स्किन in the body.
फर is घना hair.

Following the outbreak of संसार War I in 1914, the German Army खोली the Western सामने by first आक्रमणकारी Luxembourg और Belgium, then gaining military कंट्रोल of important औद्योगिक regions in France.
the tide of the advance was dramatically turned with the Battle of the Marne.
Following the रेस to the sea, both sides dug in along a meandering लकीर of fortified trenches, stretching इससे the North Sea to the Swiss frontier with France.
This line remained essentially अपरिवर्तित for most of the युद्ध.
between 1915 and 1917 वहीँ were several प्रमुख offensives साथ this सामने.
The attacks employed विशाल artillery bombardments और massed infantry अग्रिम.

In an effort to ब्रेक the deadlock, इस front saw the परिचय of new military technology, including ज़हर गैस, वायुयान and tanks.
लकिन it was तभी after the adoption of improved tactics कि कुछ degree of mobility थी restored.
the जर्मनी वसन्त अप्रिय of 1918 थी made possible by the Treaty of Brest-Litovsk कि चिह्नित the समाप्त of the conflict on the Eastern सामने.

In spite of the generally stagnant nature of this सामने, this थिएटर would prove निर्णायक.

प्रत्येक section of वास्तविक चढ़ाई between stops at the belay stations is called a pitch.

the rope is too छोटी to do the संपूर्ण रूट in one pitch ( necessity ).

the at sign @ is भी commonly called the at प्रतीक, ampersat, apetail or commercial at in English—and कम commonly a चौड़ी दायरा of other terms.
the फैक्ट कि there is no single शब्द in English लिये the प्रतीक रै prompted कुछ writers to use the फ्रेंच arobase or स्पेनी and पुर्तगाली arroba—or to coin नई शब्द such as asperand, ampersat—but none of ये रै हासिल चौड़ी करेंसी.

Mechanical मरम्मत
Maintenance, repair, and परिचालन ( MRO ) or maintenance, repair, और overhaul involves फिक्सिंग कोई sort of mechanical, plumbing or विद्युत device should it become आउट of order or broken ( known as मरम्मत, unscheduled or casualty maintenance ).
It also शामिल performing routine क्रियाएँ जिससे रखना the device in working order ( ज्ञात as scheduled maintenance ) or prevent ट्रबल from arising ( preventive maintenance ).
MRO may be पारिभाषित as, `` All actions which have the उद्देश्य of retaining or restoring an item in or to a राज्य in which it can perform its required फलन.
the क्रियाएँ include the संयोजन of all तकनीकी और सम्बन्धित प्रशासनिक, managerial, और supervision क्रियाएँ. ''
mro परिचालन can be categorised by whether the product remains the प्रॉपर्टी of the ग्राहक, i.e. a सेवा is being offered, or whether the product is bought by the reprocessing संगठन and बेची to कोई ग्राहक wishing to make the खरीदें ( Guadette, 2002 ).
In the पूर्व मामला it may be a backshop operation within a larger संगठन or smaller आपरेशन.
the former of these represents a closed लूप सप्लाई chain and usually रै the scope of मेंटेनेंस, repair or of the product.
the latter of the categorisations is an खोलें लूप supply chain and is typified by refurbishment and remanufacture.
the main characteristic of the closed लूप system is that the माँग for a उत्पाद is matched with the सप्लाई of a प्रयुक्त product.
neglecting एसेट write-offs और असाधारण activities the total जनसांख्यिकी of the उत्पाद between the customer and the service provider remains निरंतर.

the इलेक्ट्रॉन हस्तांतरण chain in the mitochondrion is the site of oxidative phosphorylation in eukaryotes.
the NADH and succinate generated in the citric एसिड साईकिल हैं oxidized, providing energy to power ATP synthase.
photosynthetic electron transport chain of the thylakoid membrane.
An electron transport chain ( ETC ) युगल electron ट्रांसफ़र between an इलेक्ट्रॉन दाता ( ऐसे as NADH ) और an electron acceptor ( ऐसे as O2 ) साथ the ट्रांसफ़र of H+ ions ( protons ) across a झिल्ली.
the resulting electrochemical proton gradient is used to generate रासायनिक उर्जा in the रूप of एडीनोसिन ट्राइफॉस्फेट ( ATP ).
इलेक्ट्रॉन हस्तांतरण chains are the cellular mechanisms प्रयुक्त लिये extracting energy इससे sunlight in photosynthesis and also इससे redox प्रतिक्रियाएँ, such as the oxidation of sugars ( respiration ).
in chloroplasts, light drives the परिवर्तन of जल to ऑक्सीजन और nadP+ to nadph साथ transfer of H+ ions across chloroplast membranes.
In mitochondria, it is the परिवर्तन of oxygen to water, NADH to NAD+ and succinate to fumarate कि are जरूरी to generate the प्रोटॉन अनुपात.
इलेक्ट्रॉन transport जंजीरों are प्रमुख साइट of असामयिक इलेक्ट्रॉन leakage to ऑक्सीजन, generating superoxide और potentially resulting in increased oxidative तनाव.

a quasi-judicial body is an एंटिटी such as an arbitrator or tribunal board, generally of a public प्रशासनिक एजेंसी, जिससे has शक्तियां and procedures resembling those of a court of law or न्यायधीश, and जिससे is obligated to objectively determine facts और draw conclusions from उन्हें so as to provide the basis of an official action.
Such क्रियाएँ are able to उपाय a situation or impose विधिक दंड, और may affect the legal अधिकारों, कर्तव्य or privileges of विशिष्ट पार्टियों.
स्मारक of tycho ब्राहे and Johannes कॅप्लर in प्राग
Tycho ब्राहे ( 14 December 154624 अक्तूबर 1601 ), born tyge ottesen ब्राहे, was a Danish nobleman ज्ञात लिये his accurate and comprehensive astronomical and ग्रहीय observations.
he थी born in स्कैनिया, then part of डेनमार्क, now part of modern-day Sweden.
Tycho was well known in his आजीवन as an astronomer और alchemist.
In his De nova स्टेला ( On the नई star ) of 1573, he refuted the aristotelian विश्वास in an अपरिवर्तनशील celestial फ्रेम.
उसके precise माप indicated कि `` नई सितारों, '' ( stellae novae, अभी known as supernovae ) in particular that of 1572, lacked the parallax अपेक्षित in sub-lunar phenomena, और यहूद therefore नहीं `` atmospheric '' tailless धूमकेतुओं as previously believed, but were above the माहौल and moon.
using समान माप he showed कि धूमकेतुओं यहूद also not atmospheric phenomena, as previously thought, और must pass through the माना `` अपरिवर्तनीय '' celestial spheres.
As an astronomer, tycho worked to combine कया he देखी as the geometrical benefits of the Copernican system with the philosophical benefits of the Ptolemaic प्रणाली into उसके अपना model of the universe, the Tychonic system.
Furthermore, he was the last of the major naked eye खगोलशास्त्रियों, working without telescopes लिये his observations.
Tycho Brahe थी granted an estate on the island of hven और the funding to build the Uraniborg, an early शोध institute, where he built large astronomical यंत्र और took अनेक careful माप, और later stjerneborg, भूमिगत, जब he खोजा कि उसके यंत्र in the former were not sufficiently steady.
on the island ( on which he demonstrated निरंकुश character और बर्ताव toward the निवासियों ) he संस्थापित manufactories ऐसे as paper-making to provide सामग्री लिये मुद्रण his परिणाम.
After मतभिन्नता साथ the new डैनिश king ईसाई iv in 1597, he was invited by the Bohemian किंग और Holy Roman emperor Rudolph II to Prague, where he became the आधिकारिक imperial astronomer.
He निर्मित the नई observatory at benátky nad jizerou.
Here, from 1600 जबतक उसके मौत in 1601, he was assisted by Johannes कॅप्लर जो later used Tycho 's astronomical आंकड़ा to develop Kepler 's कानून of ग्रहीय गति.

अनेक लोगों were involved in the आविष्कार of रेडियो as we अभी जान it.
अनेक possible methods of wireless communication यहूद considered, including inductive और capacitive प्रेरण और transmission through the ground, however the विधि used for radio today exclusively involves the हस्तांतरण and रिसेप्शन of electromagnetic लहरें.
After early speculation on the विषय, प्रायोगिक work on the connection between electricity और magnetism began around 1820 साथ the कार्य of hans ईसाई ओर्स्टेड और जारी with the कार्य of andré-marie एम्पीयर, Joseph Henry, and माइकल Faraday.

This सिद्धान्त described the सैद्धांतिक आधार of the propagation of electromagnetic लहरें.
बाद मैक्सवेल 's सिद्धान्त was published अनेक लोगों experimented with wireless संचार, कुछ intentionally using Maxwell 's theory कुछ नहीं.

The पहला व्यवस्थित और unequivocal हस्तांतरण of EM waves was performed by Heinrich Rudolf हर्ट्ज़ and वर्णित in papers published in 1887 और 1890.
हर्ट्ज़ famously considered these results as होने of little practical मान.
बाद Hertz 's कार्य अनेक लोगों were शामिल in the विकास of components और theory involved with the हस्तांतरण and रिसेप्शन of electromagnetic लहरें.

स्कर्वी is a बीमारी resulting इससे a deficiency of विटामिन C, which is required for the संश्लेषण of collagen in इंसानो.
The chemical नाम for विटामिन C, ascorbic acid, is derived इससे the लैटिन नाम of scurvy, scorbutus, which also provides the क्रियाशील scorbutic ( `` of, characterized by or having to do साथ scurvy '' ).
स्कर्वी often presents itself initially as लक्षण of malaise और lethargy, followed by गठन of धब्बे on the skin, spongy मसूड़ों, and bleeding इससे the mucous झिल्लियों.
धब्बे are most abundant on the जांघों and legs, and a व्यक्ति साथ the ailment looks pale, feels उदास, and is partially immobilized.

स्कर्वी was at एक समय आम among sailors, pirates and अन्य aboard जहाजों at sea longer than perishable fruits and vegetables could be भंडारित ( subsisting बजाय only on cured and salted meats and dried दाने ) and by सैनिको similarly वंचित of ये भोजन लिये extended अवधि.
it थी वर्णित by Hippocrates ( c. 460 BC–c. 380 bc ), और हर्बल cures for स्कर्वी have been ज्ञात in अनेक देशी संस्कृतियों since prehistory.
स्कर्वी थी one of the limiting कारकों of marine सफर, often killing large numbers of the passengers और crew on long-distance voyages.
इस became a significant issue in Europe इससे the beginning of the modern era in the आयु of डिस्कवरी in the 15th century, continuing to play a significant role through संसार War i in the 20th century.
जबकि आज scurvy is ज्ञात to be caused by a nutritional deficiency, until the isolation of vitamin c और सीधा evidence of its link to scurvy in 1932, numerous theories and treatments were proposed, प्रायः on छोटी or no प्रायोगिक आंकड़ा.
इस inconsistency is attributed to the कमी of vitamin C as a पृथक अवधारणा, an अक्षमता to reliably कड़ी different foods ( notably उपस्थित in fresh citrus, watercress, और अंग मांस ) to scurvy.

however जबतक the 1930s, treatment थी inconsistent, with अनेक अप्रभावी treatments used into the 20th century.
it थी a Scottish सर्जन in the royal नेवी, जेम्स lind जो पहला proved it could be treated साथ citrus fruit in प्रयोग he वर्णित in his 1753 किताब, a Treatise of the स्कर्वी, हालांकि उसके सलाह was not implemented by the Royal नेवी for अनेक decades.

However, barlow 's disease may भी refer to mitral वाल्व prolapse.
Other eponyms लिये scurvy शामिल moeller 's बीमारी और cheadle 's disease.
स्कर्वी करता नहीं occur in most animals क्युकी they can synthesize उनके own vitamin c.
However, humans and other उच्चतर primates ( the simians - बंदरों और apes - और tarsiers ), guinea pigs, most or all bats, और some species of पक्षियों और fish lack an एंजाइम ( L-gulonolactone oxidase ) necessary लिये ऐसे संश्लेषण और जरूर obtain vitamin c through their diet.

आयरन is a रासायनिक तत्व with the symbol fe ( इससे ) और atomic number 26.
it is a मेटल in the first परिवर्तन series.
It is the most common element ( by द्रव्यमान ) forming the ग्रह धरती as a whole, forming much of Earth 's बाहरी and inner core.
it is the fourth most common element in the धरती 's क्रस्ट.
Iron 's very common presence in रॉकी planets जैसे Earth is due to its abundant उत्पादन as a परिणाम of fusion in high-mass सितारों, जहाँ the production of nickel-56 ( which decays to the most common isotope of आयरन ) is the पिछला नाभिकीय संलयन reaction कि is ऊष्माक्षेपी.
इस कल्याणकारी radioactive निकल to become the पिछला तत्व to be produced before पतन of a सुपरनोवा लीड to the विस्फोटक events that scatter this precursor radionuclide of आयरन abundantly into space.
Like other group 8 elements, आयरन exists in a wide range of ऑक्सीकरण states, −2 to +6, हालांकि +2 और +3 are the most common.
elemental iron occurs in meteoroids and अन्य कम ऑक्सीजन environments, but is reactive to ऑक्सीजन और जल.
Fresh iron surfaces appear lustrous silvery-gray, लकिन oxidize in normal एयर to give hydrated iron आक्साइड, commonly known as चढ़.
नापसंद अनेक other metals which रूप passivating ऑक्साइड layers, आयरन oxides occupy अधिक आवाज़ than आयरन metal, and यूँ आयरन आक्साइड फ्लेक off और expose भैस surfaces लिये संक्षारण.
आयरन metal has महरूम used चूंकि प्राचीन times, though तांबे alloys, which have lower melting temperatures, were used पहला in इतिहास.
pure iron is soft ( softer than एल्युमिनियम ), लकिन is unobtainable by smelting.
the सामग्री is significantly hardened और strengthened by impurities from the smelting प्रक्रम, ऐसे as कार्बन.
A निश्चित proportion of carbon ( between 0.002 % और 2.1 % ) produces स्टील, which may be up to 1000 टाइम्स harder than pure iron.

further refinement साथ ऑक्सीजन reduces the carbon content to the सही proportion to मेक स्टील.
Steels और कम कार्बन iron alloys with other metals ( alloy steels ) are by दूर the most common metals in industrial उपयोग, due to their ग्रेट दायरा of desirable properties और the प्रचुरता of आयरन.
Iron रासायनिक compounds, जिससे शामिल अमिश्रित और ferric यौगिकों, have many uses.
आयरन ऑक्साइड मिश्रित with एल्युमिनियम चूर्ण can be ignited to बनाएँ a थर्माइट reaction, प्रयुक्त in welding and purifying ores.
It फ़ॉर्म शब्दकोष यौगिकों with the हैलोजन्स और the chalcogens.
among its कार्बधातुक यौगिकों is ferrocene, the पहला sandwich यौगिक discovered.
आयरन plays an महत्वपूर्ण role in जीवविज्ञान, forming देवालय with molecular oxygen in हीमोग्लोबिन और myoglobin ; ये दो यौगिकों are आम oxygen हस्तांतरण proteins in vertebrates.

The chernobyl disaster (, Chornobylska Katastrofa – Chornobyl Catastrophe ) थी a catastrophic नाभिकीय accident that occurred on 26 अप्रैल 1986 at the Chernobyl नाभिकीय शक्ति संयंत्र in Ukraine ( तब officially the यूक्रेनी ssr ), जिससे was under the सीधा jurisdiction of the सेंट्रल अधिकारियों of the Soviet Union.

the बैटल to contain the contamination और avert a वृहद प्रलय ultimately involved over 500,000 workers और लागत an अनुमानित 18 अरब rubles.

It scans a user 's computer quickly, and प्रदर्शक browser hijacking locations, showing what प्रविष्टियां हैं वहीँ.

on फ़रवरी 16, 2012, Trend सूक्ष्म released the hijackthis source code as खोलें source और it is अभी available on the SourceForge site.

Notice of स्टैम्प Act of 1765 in Newspaper
अमरीकी अखबारों reacted to the स्टैम्प Act with anger और पूर्वानुमान of the demise of journalism.
The स्टैम्प Act 1765 ( short शीर्षक Duties in American colonies अधिनियम 1765 ; 5 George III, c. 12 ) imposed a सीधा कर by the अंग्रेजों पार्लियामेंट specifically on the colonies of अंग्रेजों अमेरिका, और it required that अनेक printed materials in the colonies be उत्पादित on stamped पेपर produced in लंदन, carrying an embossed revenue stamp.
ये मुद्रित materials were विधिक documents, मैगज़ीन, newspapers and अनेक अन्य प्रकार of paper प्रयुक्त throughout the colonies.
जैसे पिछला taxes, the स्टैम्प कर था to be सशुल्क in मान्य British करेंसी, नहीं in colonial paper धन.
The purpose of the कर was to help pay लिये सैनिकों stationed in North अमेरिका बाद the अंग्रेजों victory in the सात Years ' War.
the British सरकारी felt that the colonies were the प्राथमिक beneficiaries of इस सैन्य उपस्थिति, and चाहिए pay at तनिक a portion of the expense.
The स्टैम्प अधिनियम मिले great प्रतिरोध in the colonies.
The colonies sent no representatives to Parliament, और इसलिए had no influence over what कर were उठाया, कैसा वे were levied, or how they would be spent.
Many colonists माना it a उल्लंघन of their rights as अंग्रेजो to be taxed without उनके consent —consent that तभी the औपनिवेशिक legislatures could ग्रान्ट.
औपनिवेशिक assemblies भेजा petitions and विरोध.
the Stamp Act Congress आयोजित in New York City, reflecting the पहला significant joint औपनिवेशिक response to any अंग्रेजों माप, भी petitioned Parliament and the किंग.
Local विरोध groups, led by colonial merchants और landowners, स्थापित connections through पत्राचार that created a loose coalition that extended इससे New इंग्लैण्ड to Georgia.
Protests and demonstrations initiated by the Sons of स्वतंत्रता प्रायः turned violent and destructive as the masses became शामिल.
बहुत जल्द सब स्टैम्प tax distributors were सहमे into resigning their commissions, और the कर थी never effectively एकत्रित.
विपक्ष to the स्टैम्प अधिनियम was not सीमित to the colonies.
British merchants और manufacturers, whose निर्यात to the colonies यहूद threatened by औपनिवेशिक economic समस्याएं exacerbated by the कर, also pressured पार्लियामेंट.
the अधिनियम थी repealed on कूच 18, 1766 as a पदार्थ of expedience, लकिन Parliament affirmed इसके शक्ति to legislate लिये the colonies “in सब cases whatsoever” by भी गुजर the Declaratory Act.
वहीँ followed a series of new कर और regulations, likewise opposed by the colonists.
The episode played a प्रमुख भूमिका in धमक the grievances और enabling the व्यवस्थित औपनिवेशिक resistance कि led to the American Revolution in 1775.

PT नौकाएँ were a variety of torpedo-armed fast आक्रमण शिल्प used by the संयुक्त राज्य नेवी in संसार War ii to आक्रमण larger surface ships.
`` PT '' is the us hull classification symbol लिये `` पैट्रोल Torpedo ''.
The pt नाव squadrons were nicknamed `` the mosquito बेड़े ''.
The जापानी पुकारा them `` Devil नौकाएँ ''.
the original pre– World War I torpedo boats यहूद designed with `` displacement '' hulls.
वे विस्थापित up to 300 tons और the शीर्ष गति थी.
The pt boats used in संसार युद्ध II were built using the planing -type हल रूप विकसित लिये रेसिंग नौकाएँ.
They were much छोटी ( 30–75 tons ) और तेज़ ( 35–40 knots ).
दोनो प्रकार यहूद designed to strike at larger warships साथ torpedoes, using relatively ऊँची speed to मिलेंगी close, and छोटी आकार to avoid being spotted और hit by gunfire.
वे यहूद much कम expensive than विशाल warships.
pt boats यहूद much तेज़, छोटी, and सस्ता than conventional ( विस्थापन hull ) vessels.
दौरान World War II, American PT boats सगाई enemy destroyers और numerous other सतह शिल्प, ranging इससे small नौकाएँ to large सप्लाई ships.
pt नौकाएँ also संचालित as gunboats विरूद्ध enemy छोटी शिल्प, such as कराया barges used by the जापानी forces for inter-island हस्तांतरण.
शुभ Friday is a धार्मिक holiday observed primarily by ईसाइयों commemorating the crucifixion of Jesus Christ और his मौत at Calvary.
The holiday is observed दौरान पावन सप्ताह as part of the paschal Triduum on the शुक्रवार preceding Easter Sunday, and may coincide with the यहूदी observance of passover.
It is also ज्ञात as पावन Friday, Great Friday, Black शुक्रवार, or ईस्टर शुक्रवार, हालांकि the latter properly refers to the Friday in Easter week.
Based on the विवरण of the canonical gospels, the Crucifixion of Jesus थी सबसे संभावित to have महरूम on a Friday ( the day पहले the sabbath ) ( ).

a third विधि, using a completely अलग खगोलीय approach based on a lunar crucifixion अंधेरा and ग्रहण मॉडल ( सतत with apostle Peter 's सन्दर्भ to a `` moon of रक्त '' in Acts 2:20 ), points to शुक्रवार, 3 April AD 33.

It is noted for दोनो its arid शर्तें और its जलाशय and range स्थलाकृति कि varies from the उत्तर अमरीकी कम point at Badwater Basin to the highest पाइंट of the contiguous संयुक्त राज्य, less than दूर at the summit of माउंट व्हिटनी.

The आक्रमण on पर्ल Harbor ( called हवाई आपरेशन or आपरेशन ai by the Japanese इम्पीरियल सामान्य मुख्यालय ( आपरेशन z in नियोजन ) and the Battle of Pearl हार्बर ) was a surprise सैन्य strike conducted by the इम्पीरियल Japanese नेवी against the संयुक्त States naval base at पर्ल Harbor, Hawaii, on the morning of दिसम्बर 7, 1941 ( दिसम्बर 8 in जापानी ).
इससे the standpoint of the defenders, the attack commenced at 7:48 a.m. हवाई Time.
The attack थी intended as a preventive कार्रवाई in order to रखना the u.S. प्रशांत Fleet from दखल with सैन्य क्रियाएँ the Empire of जापानी थी planning in southeast Asia विरूद्ध विदेशी territories of the संयुक्त Kingdom, the Netherlands, और the संयुक्त States.
the base was attacked by 353 जापानी fighters, bombers and torpedo planes in दो लहरें, शुभारम्भ from six aircraft carriers.
सब आठ u.S. नेवी battleships were क्षतिग्रस्त, साथ four being sunk.
दो of ये यहूद बाद raised, और साथ the बाकी four repaired, six battleships returned to सेवा later in the war.
The Japanese भी sank or damaged three cruisers, तीन destroyers, an anti-aircraft training ship, और one minelayer.
188 u.S. aircraft यहूद नष्ट ; 2,402 अमेरिकी were killed और 1,282 wounded.
Important आधार संस्थापना such as the power station, डॉकयार्ड, मेंटेनेंस, और fuel and torpedo storage facilities, as well as the submarine पियर और headquarters building ( भी home of the intelligence section ) were नहीं attacked.
Japanese नुकसान were लाइट : 29 वायुयान and पाँच midget submarines खोया, और 65 servicemen killed or wounded.
One Japanese sailor was captured.
The आक्रमण आए as a profound shock to the American लोगों and led सीधे to the अमरीकी प्रविष्टि into संसार युद्ध ii in दोनो the Pacific और यूरोपीय थिएटर.
The following day ( दिसम्बर 8 ), the संयुक्त States घोषित war on जापानी.
घरेलू support लिये non-interventionism, जिससे था been दमदार, disappeared.
Clandestine support of ब्रिटेन ( for example the Neutrality पैट्रोल ) was replaced by क्रियाशील गठबंधन.
Subsequent operations by the U.S. prompted जर्मनी और इटली to घोषित war on the u.S. on दिसम्बर 11, which was reciprocated by the U.S. the वही day.
There were numerous historical precedents लिये unannounced military action by जापानी.
However, the कमी of any औपचारिक warning, particularly while negotiations यहूद still जाहिर ongoing, led President Franklin D. रूज़वेल्ट to proclaim दिसम्बर 7, 1941, `` a तिथि which होगा live in infamy ``.

the संयुक्त राज्य अध्यक्षीय election of 1968 was the 46th quadrennial presidential election, held on मंगलवार, November 5, 1968.
the Republican nominee, former vice-president Richard Nixon, जीती the चुनाव over the लोकतांत्रिक nominee, लाज़िम vice-president ह्यूबर्ट humphrey.
Nixon भागा on a अभियान कि promised to restore law और order to the स्वदेश 's शहरों, torn by riots और crime.
Analysts have argued the election of 1968 is a realigning चुनाव as it permanently disrupted the नई सौदे Coalition कि had वर्चस्व presidential राजनीती for 36 years.
coming four years बाद Democrat lyndon B. जॉनसन जीती in a ऐतिहासिक landslide, the चुनाव saw the लाज़िम president forced out of the रेस and a रिपब्लिकन निर्वाचित लिये the पहला समय in बारह सालो.
it was a विदारक national experience, conducted दौरान a year of हिंसा कि included the assassination of सिविल rights leader Martin Luther King, jr., और subsequent रेस दंगे आरपार the nation, the assasination of Democratic presidential candidate रॉबर्ट F. A कम्पास is a navigational instrument that shows directions in a फ़्रेम of सन्दर्भ that is stationary सापेक्ष to the सतह of the earth.
The frame of सन्दर्भ defines the four cardinal directions ( or points ) – north, south, east, और west.
इंटरमीडिएट दिशानिर्देश are भी पारिभाषित.
प्रायः, a diagram पुकारा a कम्पास rose, which shows the दिशानिर्देश ( with their names प्रायः abbreviated to आद्याक्षर ), is चिह्नित on the compass.
जब the कम्पास is in उपयोग, the rose is aligned with the रियल directions in the frame of reference, so, लिये उदाहरण, the `` N '' चिह्नित on the रोज़ वाकई points to the north.
अक्सर, in addition to the rose or sometimes instead of it, angle markings in degrees are दिखाया on the compass.
North corresponds to शून्य degrees, और the angles increase clockwise, so ईस्ट is 90 degrees, दक्षिण is 180, and वेस्ट is 270.
These numbers allow the compass to दिखाएँ azimuths or bearings, which हैं commonly stated in इस संकेतन.
the चुम्बकीय कम्पास थी पहला invented as a device for divination as early as the Chinese Han Dynasty ( Since परिचय 206 BC ).
The कम्पास was प्रयुक्त in Song राजवंश China by the military for navigational orienteering by 1040-1044, and थी प्रयुक्त लिये मेरीटाइम navigation by 1111 to 1117.
The use of a compass is recorded in Western यूरोपीय between 1187 and 1202, और in फारस in 1232.
The शुष्क compass थी invented in यूरोपीय around 1300.
This was supplanted in the early 20th सदी by the liquid-filled magnetic कम्पास.

the गुर्दे हैं organs that serve several अनिवार्य नियामक roles in सबसे पशु, सहित vertebrates और कुछ invertebrates.
वे are अनिवार्य in the urinary system और also serve homeostatic functions such as the विनियमन of electrolytes, maintenance of acid–base balance, और regulation of रक्त pressure ( via maintaining नमक and water संतुलन ).
वे serve the body as a natural फिल्टर of the blood, और remove wastes which हैं diverted to the urinary bladder.
In producing urine, the गुर्दे excrete wastes ऐसे as urea and ammonium, और वे are also जिम्मेदार लिये the reabsorption of जल, ग्लूकोज, and amino acids.

Located at the rear of the abdominal गुहा in the retroperitoneum, the गुर्दे प्राप्त blood from the paired renal arteries, and नाली into the paired renal रगों.

Diseases of the गुर्दा हैं विविध, लकिन individuals साथ kidney बीमारी अक्सर display characteristic clinical features.
Common clinical conditions involving the गुर्दा include the nephritic and nephrotic syndromes, renal cysts, अधि kidney चोट, दीर्घकालिक गुर्दा बीमारी, urinary tract संक्रमण, nephrolithiasis, and urinary tract obstruction.
Various cancers of the गुर्दा exist ; the सबसे आम वयस्क renal कर्कट is renal cell कार्सिनोमा.

When renal फलन, measured by glomerular filtration rate, is persistently poor, dialysis and kidney प्रत्यारोपण may be treatment विकल्प.
हालांकि वे हैं नहीं severely नुकसानदेह, kidney stones can be painful और a nuisance.
The removal of kidney stones involves अल्ट्रासाउंड उपचार to break up the पत्थरों into smaller टुकड़े, जिससे are तब passed through the urinary ट्रैक्ट.

लापरवाही ( Lat. negligentia, from neglegere, to उपेक्षा, literally `` not to चुनें up something '' ) is a विफलता to exercise the परवाह that a reasonably दूरदर्शी person होता exercise in like हालातों.
the क्षेत्रफल of tort law known as लापरवाही involves नुक़सान caused by carelessness, नहीं जानबूझकर नुक़सान.
According to Jay M. feinman of the rutgers University स्कूल of विधि ;
`` The कोर idea of negligence is that लोगों चाहिए कसरत reasonable परवाह when वे अधिनियम by taking account of the potential harm that वे might foreseeably cause नुक़सान to अन्य लोगों. ''
`` those who go personally or लाओ प्रॉपर्टी where वे जान that वे or it may आइये into टक्कर साथ the व्यक्तियों or प्रॉपर्टी of others have by law a duty डाल upon them to use उचित परवाह and skill to avoid such a collision. ''
Fletcher v Rylands ( [ 1866 ] lr 1 ex 265 )
Through civil वाद, if an घायल व्यक्ति proves that another व्यक्ति acted negligently to cause their injury, they can recover damages to compensate for their नुक़सान.
Proving a मामला लिये लापरवाही can potentially entitle the घायल plaintiff to compensation लिये नुक़सान to उनके देह, प्रॉपर्टी, दिमागी well-being, financial status, or अंतरंग संबंध.
however, क्युकी लापरवाही मामले are बहुत fact-specific, this सामान्य परिभाषा does not fully बताइये the concept of when the law होगा आवश्यकता one person to compensate another for नुकसान caused by accidental चोट.
further, the law of negligence at common law is तभी one aspect of the विधि of liability.
Although resulting damages जरूर be सिद्ध in अनुक्रम to recover मुआवजे in a लापरवाही कार्रवाई, the nature और extent of those damages are नहीं the प्राथमिक focus of negligence cases.
A melanocytic nevus ( भी known as `` Nevocytic nevus '' ) is a type of lesion कि contains nevus cells ( a type of melanocyte ).

A mole can be either subdermal ( under the स्किन ) or a pigmented growth on the स्किन, formed ज़्यादातर of a प्रकार of कोशिका known as a melanocyte.

The व्यापक metabolic फलक, or chemical स्क्रीन, ( CMP ; CPT कोड 80053 ) is a panel of 14 रक्त परीक्षण which serves as an initial व्यापक medical स्क्रीनिंग tool.
The cmp provides a rough जाँच of गुर्दा फलन, liver फलन, and electrolyte and fluid संतुलन, लकिन it is दूर इससे perfect.
Abnormal values from a CBC may be a result of false positives और thus the cbc may need to be repeated लिये a patient ( or replaced with a अधिक विशिष्ट test ).
The cmp is an विस्तारित संस्करण of the मौलिक metabolic panel ( bmp ), which करता not include liver परीक्षण.
A CMP ( or bmp ) can be ordered as part of a दिनचर्या शारीरिक examination, or may be used to मॉनिटर a patient साथ a chronic disease, such as मधुमेह mellitus or hypertension.

the परीक्षण are performed on machines आधारित on the autoanalyzer invented in 1957.

प्राकृतिक गैस is a naturally occurring hydrocarbon gas mixture consisting primarily of methane, but commonly सहित varying amounts of other hydrocarbons, कार्बन dioxide, nitrogen, and hydrogen sulfide.
Natural gas is an energy सोर्स often used लिये हीटिंग, कुकिंग, और electricity पीढी.
It is also used as fuel for vehicles और as a रासायनिक feedstock in the manufacture of प्लास्टिक and other commercially महत्वपूर्ण सशुल्क रसायन.
प्राकृतिक gas is मिला in deep भूमिगत प्राकृतिक rock formations or associated with अन्य hydrocarbon reservoirs in कोयले beds और as मिथेन clathrates.
पेट्रोलियम is also another संसाधन मिला in निकटता to and साथ natural गैस.
सबसे प्राकृतिक gas थी निर्मित over समय by two mechanisms : biogenic and thermogenic.
biogenic गैस is created by methanogenic organisms in marshes, bogs, landfills, and shallow sediments.
Deeper in the earth, at वृहद तापमान और pressure, thermogenic gas is created from दफ्न सशुल्क सामग्री.
Before natural गैस can be प्रयुक्त as a ईंधन, it जरूर undergo प्रसंस्करण to remove impurities, सहित जल, to मिलें the specifications of marketable natural gas.
The by-products of processing शामिल ethane, प्रोपेन, butanes, pentanes, और higher आणविक weight hydrocarbons, हाइड्रोजन sulfide ( जिससे may be परिवर्तित into pure गंधक ), कार्बन डाइऑक्साइड, water वाष्प, and sometimes helium और नाइट्रोजन.
प्राकृतिक गैस is प्रायः informally referred to बस as gas, especially जब compared to other उर्जा स्त्रोत such as oil or coal.

the platypus ( ornithorhynchus anatinus ) is a semiaquatic स्तनधारी endemic to पूर्वी ऑस्ट्रेलिया, सहित तस्मानिया.
साथ साथ the four प्रजाति of echidna, it is one of the पाँच extant प्रजाति of monotremes, the only mammals that lay eggs instead of giving जनम.
It is the sole जीना प्रतिनिधि of इसके परिवार ( ornithorhynchidae ) और genus ( ornithorhynchus ), हालांकि a क्रमांक of सम्बन्धित प्रजाति have been मिला in the चट्टान रिकार्ड.
the unusual appearance of this egg-laying, बतख -billed, beaver -tailed, otter -footed स्तनधारी baffled European naturalists when वे first encountered it, साथ some considering it an elaborate fraud.
it is one of the few venomous स्तनधारियों, the male platypus having a spur on the hind पैर that delivers a venom capable of causing severe pain to humans.

The platypus is the animal emblem of the राज्य of New South Wales.
जबतक the early 20th सदी, it was hunted for its fur, लकिन it is now सुरक्षित throughout its दायरा.

थर्मल सुकून is the कंडीशन of दिमाग that expresses संतोष साथ the थर्मल पर्यावरण and is assessed by subjective मूल्यांकन ( ansi / ASHRAE Standard 55 ).
maintaining इस मानक of thermal comfort लिये occupants of buildings or other enclosures is एक of the महत्वपूर्ण goals of hvac ( heating, वेंटिलेशन, और air conditioning ) डिज़ाइन engineers.
The पूर्वानुमानित औसत vote ( pmv ) मॉडल stands among the most पहचाना thermal comfort models.
It थी developed using सिद्धान्त of heat balance और प्रायोगिक data एकत्रित in a नियंत्रित climate कक्ष अंतर्गत steady राज्य conditions.
Because the pmv मॉडल was derived from आंकड़ा एकत्रित in a controlled जलवायु, it is नहीं उपयुक्त for अनुप्रयोग in naturally ventilated spaces which प्रायः have ऊँची स्तर of air movement.
इस shortcoming motivated the विकास of a family of empirical statistical models of thermal सुकून in naturally ventilated स्पेसेस known as adaptive मॉडल.
अनुकूली models of थर्मल सुकून consider occupants as dynamically interacting साथ उनके environment, and controlling their thermal comfort by means of कपडे or window-opening और closing.
इस is in कंट्रास्ट to thermal सुकून in sealed buildings, in जिससे occupants अनुभव the पर्यावरण passively.
Thermal सुकून is affected by heat conduction, convection, radiation, and evaporative heat loss.
Thermal comfort is maintained जब the heat उत्पन्न by human चयापचय is अनुमत to dissipate, thus maintaining thermal संतुलन साथ the surroundings.
It has महरूम long पहचाना कि the सनसनी of feeling hot or cold is not just dependent on air तापमान अलोन.
Thermal सुकून calculations according to ANSI/ASHRAE Standard 55 can be freely performed साथ the CBE Thermal Comfort Tool लिये ashrae-55.

In 1985, जब Dunlop Rubber थी taken over by btr plc, the कम्पनी acquired the ऑटोमोबाइल tire assets of dunlop, including the right to use the dunlop brand on ऑटोमोबाइल tires.

the Alps हैं one of the great पहाड़ दायरा systems of Europe stretching approximately आरपार आठ Alpine countries from ऑस्ट्रिया and Slovenia in the ईस्ट, स्विट्ज़रलैंड, liechtenstein, Germany, France to the वेस्ट and इटली और Monaco to the दक्षिण.
The mountains were formed over hundreds of लाखो of सालो as the अफ़्रीकी and Eurasian tectonic प्लेटों collided.
Extreme shortening caused by the इवेंट resulted in marine sedimentary रॉक्स उठती by thrusting और folding into high पहाड़ peaks such as मोंट blanc and the matterhorn.
मोंट blanc spans the french–italian border, और at is the उच्चतम mountain in the Alps.
the अल्पाइन प्रदेश क्षेत्रफल contains many चोटियों उच्चतर than, known as the `` four-thousanders ``.
The ऊँचाई और आकार of the दायरा affects the climate in Europe ; in the kyu वर्षण स्तर vary greatly and climatic शर्तें consist of distinct zones.
वन्यजीव ऐसे as ibex live in the उच्चतर peaks to elevations of, and पौधे ऐसे as edelweiss grow in rocky क्षेत्रों in lower elevations as खूब as in higher elevations.
Evidence of human habitation in the Alps goes back to the Paleolithic era.
A mummified man, संकल्पित to be 5,000 सालो old, थी discovered on a glacier at the austrian–italian border in 1991.
by the 6th सदी BC, the सेल्टिक La tène culture थी well established.
Hannibal may have crossed the ऐल्प्स with a झुंड of हाथियों, and the romans था settlements in the region.
In 1800 नेपोलियन crossed one of the पहाड़ गुजरता with an army of 40,000.
The 18th and 19th सदियां saw an influx of naturalists, लेखक, और कलाकारों, in particular the Romantics, followed by the golden आयु of alpinism as mountaineers began to ascend the peaks.
In संसार युद्ध II the Third Reich invaded the Alpine देशों, with the एक्सेप्शन of स्विट्ज़रलैंड and Liechtenstein ; Adolf Hitler kept a आधार of आपरेशन in the bar ऐल्प्स throughout the war.
the Alpine region has a strong सांस्कृतिक identity.
The traditional संस्कृति of खेती, cheesemaking, और woodworking स्टिल exists in Alpine villages, although the tourist industry began to grow early in the 20th सदी and विस्तारित greatly बाद संसार War II to become the प्रबल उद्योग by the समाप्त of the सदी.
The Winter ओलम्पिक खेल have महरूम hosted in the Swiss, फ्रेंच, इतालवी, आस्ट्रिया and German Alps.
at present the प्रदेश is घर to 14 million लोगों and has 120 million annual visitors.

परिवार हस्तांतरण of बास्क भाषा ( Basque as initial language )
प्रतिशत of विद्यार्थी पंजीकृत in Basque language schools ( 2000–2005 ).
स्थान of the Basque-language प्रांतों within Spain and France
बास्क ( endonym :, ) is the ancestral language of the Basque लोगों, जो inhabit the Basque देश, a प्रदेश spanning an area in northeastern स्पेन and southwestern France.
It is बोला by 27 % of basques in सब territories ( 714,136 आउट of 2,648,998 ).
Of ये, 663,035 live in the Spanish part of the Basque देश and the remaining 51,100 सजीव in the French भाग.
In अकादमिक discussions of the वितरण of Basque in Spain और France, it is customary to refer to तीन ancient provinces in फ़्रांस और four Spanish provinces.
Native अध्यक्षों हैं concentrated in a संलग्न area सहित भाग of the स्पेनी autonomous communities of the Basque Country और नावारा और in the पश्चिमी half of the French département of pyrénées-atlantiques.
the बास्क autonomous Community is an administrative entity within the binational ethnographic Basque देश incorporating the traditional Spanish प्रांतों of Biscay, Gipuzkoa, और álava, जिससे retain उनके अस्तित्व as politico-administrative विभाजन.
These प्रांतों और अनेक क्षेत्रों of नावारा हैं heavily आबादी by ethnic Basques, but बास्क थी, at least जबतक the 1990s, not spoken as a native language in सबसे of álava, पश्चिमी parts of Biscay और central and दक्षिणी क्षेत्रों of Navarre, either क्युकी it था महरूम replaced by स्पेनी along the सदियां, in कुछ क्षेत्रों, or because it had never महरूम बोला there, in other क्षेत्रों.
in southwestern France, the ancient Basque-populated provinces यहूद labourd, Lower नावारा, and soule.
They and अन्य regions यहूद संचित into a single département in 1790 अंतर्गत the नाम Basses-Pyrénées, a name जिससे persisted जबतक 1970.
A मानकीकृत form of the बास्क language, पुकारा Euskara batua, was विकसित by the बास्क भाषा Academy in the लेट 1960s.
Euskara batua थी created so कि बास्क language could be used—and easily समझा by सब Basque speakers—in औपचारिक situations ( शिक्षा, mass media, साहित्य ), और this is its main use today.
The भूमिका of इस मानक Basque भाषा depends on the linguistic शैक्षणिक मॉडल of प्रत्येक प्रदेश and each स्कूल.
In सबसे areas of the स्पेनी बास्क Country, the शैक्षणिक Model D, जहाँ all subjects हैं taught in Basque, except `` Spanish भाषा and साहित्य '' ( जिससे is taught in स्पेनी ) is now the predominant मॉडल.
in France, the बास्क भाषा school seaska and the association लिये a bilingual ( Basque and French ) schooling Ikasbi मिलें a चौड़ी range of बास्क language educational needs up to the Sixth Form, जबकि प्रायः struggling to surmount वित्तीय और administrative constraints.
अलावा from this मानकीकृत संस्करण, वहीँ are five प्रमुख बास्क dialects : Bizkaian, gipuzkoan, और Upper Navarrese in Spain, and navarrese–lapurdian और Zuberoan ( in फ़्रांस ).
हालांकि they take उनके names इससे the mentioned ऐतिहासिक प्रांतों, the dialect boundaries हैं नहीं congruent with प्रांत boundaries.

A दिए नाम, in Western contexts प्रायः referred to as a first name, is a personal name कि specifies and differentiates between members of a group of individuals, especially in a family, सब of जिनकी members usually share the same family name ( उपनाम ).

हाइड्रोक्लोरिक acid is a साफ, colourless solution of hydrogen chloride ( h cl ) in जल.
it is a अत्यधिक क्षयकारी, strong खनिज acid with many औद्योगिक उपयोग.
हाइड्रोक्लोरिक एसिड is found naturally in gastric एसिड.
Historically called muriatic एसिड, and spirits of नमक, हाइड्रोक्लोरिक एसिड was produced from vitriol ( sulfuric acid ) और आम नमक.
it पहला appeared during the Renaissance, और तब it थी used by chemists such as glauber, Priestley and डेवी in their scientific research.
With प्रमुख production starting in the Industrial क्रान्ति, हाइड्रोक्लोरिक acid is used in the chemical industry as a chemical अभिकर्मक in the large-scale production of विनाइल chloride for पीवीसी प्लास्टिक, और MDI / tdi for polyurethane.
It has numerous smaller-scale अनुप्रयोग, including household cleaning, production of gelatin and other food additives, descaling, and चमड़े processing.

Wheat ( triticum spp. ) is a खाद्यान्न grain, originally इससे the levant region of the Near East and Ethiopian हाइलैंड्स, but now cultivated worldwide.
In 2010, संसार उत्पादन of wheat was 651 million tons, making it the तीसरा most-produced cereal बाद maize ( 844 million टन ) और rice ( 672 लाख tons ).
Wheat was the दूसरी most-produced खाद्यान्न in 2009 ; world उत्पादन in that साल थी 682 million tons, बाद मक्का ( 817 million टन ), और with राइस as a close third ( 679 million टन ).
इस अनाज is grown on अधिक land क्षेत्रफल than कोई other commercial food.
संसार trade in wheat is greater than लिये सब other फसलों संयुक्त.
globally, गेहूं is the leading source of vegetable protein in इंसान food, having a higher protein content than soybeans or the other प्रमुख cereals, मक्का ( मकई ) or राइस.
in terms of कुल production tonnages प्रयुक्त लिये food, it is currently second to rice as the प्रमुख human food क्रॉप and ahead of maize, बाद allowing for maize 's अधिक extensive use in एनिमल फ़ीड्स.
गेहूं was a key factor enabling the emergence of city-based societies at the start of सभ्यता because it was एक of the पहला crops कि could be easily cultivated on a large scale, and had the additional लाभ of yielding a कटाई that provides long-term storage of खाना.
Wheat contributed to the emergence of city-states in the Fertile crescent, सहित the Babylonian और Assyrian empires.
गेहूं grain is a staple खाना used to make आटा for leavened, flat और steamed breads, बिस्कुट, कुकीज़, cakes, breakfast खाद्यान्न, pasta, noodles, couscous and for fermentation to मेक beer, अन्य alcoholic पेय, or biofuel.
गेहूं is planted to a सीमित extent as a forage crop for पशुधन, and इसके straw can be प्रयुक्त as a construction सामग्री for roofing thatch.
The whole अनाज can be milled to leave बस the भ्रूणपोष लिये श्वेत आटा.
The by-products of this are चोकर और germ.
the whole grain is a concentrated source of विटामिन, minerals, and protein, जबकि the refined grain is mostly starch.

the प्रतिष्ठित Eightfold Path (, ) is एक of the प्रिंसिपल शिक्षाओं of the Buddha, जो वर्णित it as the रास्ता अग्रणी to the cessation of suffering ( dukkha ) and the उपलब्धि of self-awakening.
it is used to develop insight into the true nature of phenomena ( or reality ) और to eradicate लोभ, hatred, and delusion.
the प्रतिष्ठित eightfold Path is the चौथी of the Buddha 's चार प्रतिष्ठित सच्चाई ; the first element of the Noble Eightfold पाथ is, in फेरे, an understanding of the Four Noble Truths.
it is also ज्ञात as the मध्य पाथ or मध्य रास्ता.
सब eight elements of the पाथ begin साथ the शब्द `` सही '', which translates the word samyañc ( in संस्कृत ) or sammā ( in Pāli ).
ये denote completion, togetherness, और coherence, और can भी सुझाएँ the senses of `` perfect '' or `` ideal ''.
'Samma ' is भी translated as `` wholesome '', `` हिकमत '' और `` skillful ''.
in Buddhist प्रतीकवाद, the प्रतिष्ठित eightfold Path is प्रायः represented by अर्थात् of the dharma wheel ( dharmachakra ), जिनकी आठ spokes represent the आठ elements of the पाथ.

अर्थशास्त्र is the social विज्ञान that analyzes the production, distribution, and consumption of goods and सेवाएं.
the पद economics आता from the प्राचीन यूनानी ( ', `` management of a household, प्रशासन '' ) from ( ', `` हाउस '' ) + ( ', `` कस्टम '' or `` law '' ), hence `` rules of the house ( hold ) ''.
राजनैतिक अर्थव्यवस्था थी the पहले name for the subject, लकिन अर्थशास्त्रियों in the late 19th century suggested `` economics '' as a shorter term for `` आर्थिक विज्ञान '' that also avoided a narrow political-interest connotation and as similar in form to `` गणित ``, `` ethics '', और so forth.
A focus of the subject is कैसा economic agents behave or interact और how economies work.
Consistent साथ this, a primary textbook भेद is between microeconomics और macroeconomics.
Microeconomics examines the behavior of मौलिक तत्व in the अर्थव्यवस्था, including individual agents ( ऐसे as households and firms or as buyers and विक्रेता ) और बाज़ार, और their interactions.
Macroeconomics analyzes the entire economy और issues affecting it, सहित बेरोजगारी, inflation, आर्थिक growth, and monetary and फिस्कल policy.
अन्य व्यापक भेद include those between positive अर्थशास्त्र ( describing `` what is '' ) and normative अर्थशास्त्र ( advocating `` what ought to be '' ) ; between economic theory और लागू economics ; between rational और behavioral economics ; और between मुख्यधारा economics ( more `` orthodox '' and dealing with the `` rationality-individualism-equilibrium nexus '' ) और शास्त economics ( more `` कट्टरपंथी '' और dealing साथ the `` institutions-history-social ढांचा नेक्सस '' ).
Economic विश्लेषण may be लागू throughout society, as in business, finance, स्वास्थ्य care, और सरकारी, लकिन also to such diverse विषय as crime, education, the परिवार, law, राजनीती, religion, सोशल institutions, war, and science.
At the turn of the 21st century, the expanding domain of economics in the सोशल sciences has महरूम described as economic साम्राज्यवाद.
An increasing क्रमांक of economists have called for increased जोर on environmental स्थिरता ; इस area of research is known as ecological अर्थशास्त्र.

Section 8 of the आवास Act of 1937 ( ), often बस known as खण्ड 8, as repeatedly amended, authorizes the भुगतान of rental आवास assistance to private landlords on निमित्त of approximately 3.1 million low-income households.

The US विभाग of आवास and Urban विकास manages the Section 8 programs.
the आवास चुनाव Voucher कार्यक्रम provides `` tenant-based '' rental सहायता, so a किरायेदार can move इससे one ईकाई of at least न्यूनतम housing quality to another.

a किरायेदार who पत्ते a subsidized प्रोजेक्ट होगा lose अभिगम to the project-based रियायत.
